In the last two years, business has gradually declined due to the global economic downturn and the sharp drop in the price of silver, as well as the excessively high freight rates of the South Manchuria Railway. As of February of this year, the total revenue reduction exceeded 27,158,061 yen. The Japanese were greatly panicked by this, blaming it on the construction of railways by our country and the reduction of freight rates for the Four-Railway Joint Transportation, and began so-called railway negotiations. The government and public clamored incessantly, all day long. They invade our land, seize our interests, and interfere with our country's transportation administration. They speak of co-existence and co-prosperity, but in reality, they strangle our throat and try to put us to death. Their strength and unreasonableness are truly beyond compare.

Since the establishment of the company's foundation, the Japanese have planned to build a South Manchurian railway network with the South Manchuria Railway as the main artery to encompass the entire Northeast region and make it inescapable. The insidious means of completing this railway network are generally:

(1) To vigorously develop Japan's existing railways and demand new railway rights to build new railways.

(2) To vigorously sabotage our country's self-operated railways. If sabotage fails, then demand investment and strive for control, so that our country has only the name while Japan controls the reality.

(3) To engage in economic competition with the Chinese Eastern Railway, loudly advocating the opening of the Northeast gateway, isolating our country diplomatically, and facilitating the implementation of its railway plans.

The so-called South Manchuria Railway as the main artery is the South Manchuria Railway centralism. The foundation of this centralism is based on the Dalian Port supremacy. If a railway does not have a seaport as its outlet, then its own value is very limited. It will inevitably become a nurturing line for railways with ports. Therefore, the Japanese have used the superior position of the South Manchuria Railway to vigorously develop its functions. On the one hand, they are expanding the throughput of Dalian Port and improving its facilities. On the other hand, they are planning to build interconnected circular railways. As for now, the Japanese focus is again concentrated on the completion of the Jihui Railway and the development of North Korean seaports. If successful, then the Japanese railways will flourish together, and multiple ports will compete for glory, advancing simultaneously from the southeast sides toward our Northeast. If their plans are realized, then their power will be like a net cast from all directions. Where can the provinces in our Northeast escape to? Therefore, the people of our country must swear to reject the Japanese demand for the construction of the Jihui Railway and should strive to complete the construction of Huludao Port. Otherwise, the future is bleak and unimaginable.

The railways currently operated by the South Manchuria Railway Company are:

(1) The South Manchuria Railway Main Line from Changchun to Dalian, a total of 438.5 miles

(2) The Anfeng Line from Sujiatun to Andong, a total of 161.7 miles

(3) The Lushun Line from Lushun to Choushui, a total of 31.6 miles

(4) The Yingkou Line from Dashiqiao to Yingkou, a total of 13.9 miles

(5) The Yantai Line from Yantai to Yantai Coal Mine, a total of 9.7 miles

(6) The Fushun Line from Yanghe to Fushun, a total of 35.4 miles, totaling 690.8 miles. Among them, the Japanese want to extend the lease period of the South Manchuria Railway and the Anfeng Railway in the twenty-one articles to ninety-nine years. The lease period of Lushun and Dalian has also been extended to ninety-nine years. They even attempt to occupy it permanently. However, our country has never recognized the twenty-one articles, and the Japanese cannot use it as an excuse. (To be continued)

Important News

The Reorganization of Shi Bu (Shi Yousan's Troops)

More than 10,000 members of Shi's troops arrived in Shandong

Shi has crossed the Jinpu Railway to leave the country

It has not yet been confirmed that Mi Wenhe has been captured

Jinan Correspondence: Soldiers from Shi Yousan's defeated troops have been arriving in Shandong in droves. This reporter visited Chairman Han Fuqu of the Shandong Provincial Government this afternoon (7th) to inquire about the number of Shi's troops who arrived in Shandong, the resettlement measures, and the whereabouts of Shi Yousan himself. According to Han, more than 10,000 troops of Shi Yousan have retreated to Shandong in recent days and are located near Dezhou and Wucheng. It is not yet known how many more will arrive. The resettlement will first involve gathering and reorganizing the troops. How they will be reorganized will depend on the number of troops that arrive. Commander-in-Chief Chiang sent a telegram to Jinan yesterday, approving a preliminary allocation of 200,000 yuan from the central government for the resettlement of Shi's troops. In the future, the military pay for the reorganized Shi's troops will be determined separately by the central government and disbursed monthly. Currently, all supplies and provisions for Shi's troops are being provided by the government. Flour, military uniforms, etc., were transported from Jinan to Shi's troops the day before yesterday. Shi Yousan's telegram announcing his resignation has already been sent out. It is reported that Shi himself has crossed east of the Jinpu Railway. There are many seaports in the vicinity, and it is likely that he will leave the country from the Yangjiaogou area and will definitely not come to Jinan. This reporter also inquired about the accuracy of the news reported in Zhang Xueliang's telegram yesterday, which stated that Mi Wenhe and Sun Guangqian had been captured. According to Han, it is likely that Sun Guangqian was captured, but it is said that Mi Wenhe has not been captured. (7th)

Ge Guangting's Discussion

Shi's Troops are in Utter Disarray

Shi's Troops are completely handed over to Han for reorganization

Vice Commander Zhang will return to Liaoning within days

Qingdao Correspondence: Ge Guangting, Chairman of the Jiaoji Railway, was ordered by Vice Commander Zhang Xueliang to remain in Jinan due to military tension in order to liaise with Shandong Chairman Han Fuqu regarding important matters. Now that Ge believes that Shi's troops have been largely resolved, and the military situation has come to an end, there is no need to remain in Jinan. Therefore, he took the Jiaoji Railway train back to Qingdao last night (6th). According to Ge's account of the truth about the resolution of Shi's troops, "After Shi's troops were attacked by the Northeast Army and the Central Army, they were in utter disarray. Approximately 20,000 people have surrendered their weapons. Furthermore, according to the telegram of victory forwarded by Vice Commander Zhang this morning from Commander Yu of the First Army Corps, the defeated enemy was ambushed by our cavalry and the South Route Army north of Shulu, and over 10,000 people surrendered their weapons. The remnants then entrenched themselves in the Fanjiazhuang, Dongxi Baying, and Shuangliushu areas and were completely surrounded by our cavalry and the South Route Army. The entire enemy was disarmed around noon. Shi's division commanders Sun Guangqian and Mi Wenhe, and others were captured. Shi Yousan only led his pistol regiment to escape towards Hengshui. Our Fifth Cavalry Brigade has been tracking and pursuing them, and the Sixth Cavalry Brigade is searching the battlefield. Moreover, Shen Ke, the former division commander of Shi's troops, has indeed surrendered to our side with his troops in Quyang and is awaiting reorganization. Therefore, there are few remaining troops of Shi Yousan. It is reported that Shi himself has arrived in Zaoqiang, and there are reports that he has arrived in Wucheng from Zaoqiang. Chairman Han has indeed received a telegram from Shi expressing his remorse and indicating that he was manipulated by others and requesting to resign, handing over all his troops to Chairman Han for reorganization. Chairman Han has already sent personnel to Dezhou, Wucheng, and other places to negotiate the reorganization of Shi's troops. As for Shi himself, if he can immediately leave the army, Chairman Han can ensure his safety and send him out of the country. As for the reports that Shi will pass through Qingdao to Dalian, that is speculation and not yet certain." Furthermore, "Shi's troops can be completely eliminated within days. It is reported that Vice Commander Zhang will return to Liaoning after Shi's troops are eliminated. I (Ge Guangting) plan to visit Zhang in Ping before Vice Commander Zhang returns to Liaoning to report on the situation in Jinan with Chairman Han and to request instructions on everything. I will probably depart within three or four days." (August 7th)

Korean Residents of Wanbaoshan

After the Ditch was Completed

Trial Impoundment Flooded More Than 100 Qing of Civilian Farmland

Japanese Police Claim They Will Leave in a Few Days

Changchun Correspondence: More than a month has passed since the Wanbaoshan Incident, and the Japanese military police still have no intention of withdrawing. We hereby record the recent situation as follows:

Conditions of the Dike and Ditch: The horizontal earth dike built by Korean farmers under the supervision of the Japanese police is approximately forty zhang wide and fifteen chi high. Willow branches are used to weave fences, which are covered with earth. A place for water to flow is left in the middle, approximately four or five chi deep. If the place for water flow is blocked with earth bags, the water level of the river inside the dike will increase and flow directly into the ditch, which is more than twenty li long. Around July 10th, the dike was completed, and a trial impoundment was carried out. The water in the ditch flowed into the paddy fields, which are located on higher ground than the surrounding area and have no place to discharge the water. More than 100 qing of nearby civilian farmland were flooded. Later, the earth bags were removed, the river level dropped, and the previously flooded fields were spared from water damage. However, the滩地 on the east bank of the river is still under water. The earth dike has sunk about one chi due to water leakage. The root of the earth dike outside the water flow area has been scoured into deep eddies. In the future, if there is a heavy rain, the earth dike will collapse. Liu Jing, the Japanese Consul in Fengtian, and five others arrived in Changchun on July 24th because they were ordered by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to investigate the situation of Korean people in the Eastern Provinces. On the 26th and 27th, they went to Wanbaoshan to conduct an on-site investigation, asking farmers about the situation of the water being diverted into the ditch and the farmland being flooded. They instructed that the ditch mouth near the river should be blocked to avoid flooding, which was implemented on July 30th. It was discovered that on June 8th, Consul Liu Jing was ordered by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to come to Changchun to investigate this matter. He stayed in Changchun for two weeks before returning to Liaoning. He was deceived and surrounded by the Japanese Consul in Changchun, Tadashige Tashiro, who acted perversely, which led to the event on July 2nd when Japanese military police machine-gunned farmers who were legitimately defending themselves. If Liu Jing had gone to conduct an on-site investigation of this case at that time, it might not have become an issue long ago.

Korean People Attempt to Plant Paddy Rice: Tadashige Tashiro, the Japanese Consul in Changchun, was muddle-headed and obstinate. In late June, when the farming season was already over, he forced the Korean people to try to plant paddy rice. The Korean people all wanted to go elsewhere to make a living. The consul ordered the guarantor not to allow them to go elsewhere. At the same time, he sent police to whip and punish them for their work. The Korean people endured and went through the motions. Without digging ponds or dividing the area, and only removing the weeds, they casually scattered the rice seeds on the barren fields. In mid-July, the rice seedlings only grew to about one inch. The weeds were about two chi deep, and the rice seedlings were all suppressed by the weeds. They have now all turned yellow and withered, which is extremely ridiculous.

The Current Situation of the Resident Japanese Police: There are currently about twenty Japanese police officers at the Majia Sentinel post on the nearby river bank. Most of the Japanese police officers going to take over the shift arrive in the morning, and the police officers being transferred back mostly arrive at night, so it is not possible to obtain the exact number. Half of the Japanese police officers live in the house with the built gun emplacement owned by the He family at the river mouth, and half are scattered in temporary shelters in the wilderness at the river mouth. They patrol the ditch line and the rice fields more than twenty li away from time to time. In the house of the landowner, Zhang Hongbin, there are only six Korean people left to cook for the Japanese police. Now that the sorghum has grown tall, and the green gauze tent is up, bandits appear from time to time. The Japanese police are all on guard and restless day and night. They are all urgently awaiting orders to return to the forcibly occupied civilian houses on the river bank of Majia Sentinel. Currently, only the He family has one house, and the He family is urging them to vacate it immediately because the women in the family have nowhere to live. According to the Japanese police, "Wait a few more days, don't worry, we will be leaving soon."

Heavy Losses to Farmland: The farmland was flooded by more than 100 qing when the water was diverted for trial purposes. Fortunately, it was only for a short time, and there was no major damage. However, the ditch crosses more than twenty li, making it inconvenient for farmers to travel to cultivate their farmland, resulting in a huge loss of time, labor, and wages. In addition, the harvest of the nearby farmland, which was previously guarded by the Japanese police and not allowed to be cultivated, has also been reduced. The nearby willow trees have been forcibly cut down completely. The affected farmers submitted a report to the Jilin Provincial Government, the Changchun Municipal Preparatory Office, and the Changchun County Government in late July, stating the previous situation and requesting negotiations for compensation. The amount of each loss will be investigated and reported later.

Japanese Secretive State: The situation of the Japanese military tents and police team in Majia Sentinel, aiming with guns in the trenches, was previously photographed and published by news reporters from our country's newspapers. The Japanese were initially pleased, but then became quite regretful. When Professor Zhang Qiyun of the Department of Geography of Nanjing Central University and others went to conduct an on-site investigation on August 1st, the three military tents were combined into one. When the team members were taking photos there, the Japanese police stopped them and said that they were afraid of being publicized by the newspapers and being blamed by Chinese and foreign public opinion. (4th)

South Manchuria

Japanese Army Summer Exercises

Violating Practice of Not Notifying in Advance

Forcing Residents Within the Line to Relocate

Andong Correspondence: The Japanese garrison troops along the South Manchuria and Anfeng lines are strategically deployed, ostensibly to protect the railways and ensure the safety of passengers, but their actual purpose is not only that. According to Japanese military regulations, they conduct military exercises in sections along the railway lines once during the summer and winter, practicing fire maneuvers and conducting group combat. However, before each march, the Japanese military commanders would notify the Chinese authorities, specify the dates of the march and the area of combat, and then announce it to local merchants and residents to avoid panic. However, this summer exercise along the South Manchuria Line, the Japanese army violated the usual practice and did not notify in advance. Suddenly, from July 22nd to the 26th, the Third Artillery Battalion of the Japanese stationed in Haicheng conducted combat exercises in the area of ​​Da Qianhucun, Lizikou, and Donggangzi in the eastern suburbs of Haicheng. The artillery fire was continuous from 7:00 AM to 8:00 PM every day, and the sound shook the fields, causing general residents to be extremely frightened. The Japanese military also used the pretext of fire drills and the danger of guns and ammunition, ordering all residents within the battle line to move to other places. Each household was given one yen per day for food expenses. The residents did not dare to resist and had to move to other places with the old and the young, no different from war refugees, wandering the roads. A farmer with the surname Wang in Da Qianhucun had scheduled to marry off his daughter on the 23rd. On that day, his whole family was evicted by the Japanese army. Before they could marry off their daughter, the whole family fled to other places. Also, an old man with the surname Li in Donggangzi Village, nearly seventy years old, had a relapse of a chronic illness that had not healed for years. The Japanese army ordered his family to carry the old man to the neighboring village on a door panel. There was also a farmer named Bai Shiwu in Lizikou, who took his wife and daughter to a neighboring village to hide. Bai accidentally walked into the Japanese battle line and was arrested by the Japanese army, beaten severely, and then released. There were several other villagers who were beaten by the Japanese army for moving too slowly or accidentally stepping into the battle line. The villagers felt uneasy. The local Public Security Bureau repeatedly reported the situation to the villagers, and after dispatching personnel to conduct an on-site investigation, they once tried to stop it, but to no avail. Therefore, they reported it to the county government, requesting negotiations with the Japanese side. The report stated that the Japanese army's live ammunition shooting outside the occupied territories was already detrimental to national dignity. Furthermore, it was even more disregard for our country's sovereignty to commit violence and injure people. If the matter is not seriously negotiated, the Japanese army will be even more unbridled in the future. However, by the time the county government raised the matter for negotiation with the Japanese side, the Japanese military's combat period had ended, and the entire team had returned to defense. (August 5th)

Unprecedented Flood in Hunan Province

Disaster-stricken Area Comprises Forty-Two Counties

Estimated Number of Deaths by Drowning Reaches Tens of Thousands

Changsha Correspondence: Since the beginning of summer in Hunan Province, it has been raining continuously for months, causing flash floods and turning the plains into rivers. Forty-two counties, including Xiangxiang and Xiangtan, have reported floods one after another. The water situation is especially severe in the counties bordering the lake. The number of deaths by drowning in each county is estimated to be in the tens of thousands, and the number of displaced people reaches hundreds of thousands. Dikes and embankments have collapsed, and crops have been submerged. The crops in the high-lying fields in each county have also been damaged by螟蟊 due to the prolonged rain, and the autumn harvest is completely hopeless. The severity of the disaster is truly unprecedented. The Provincial Relief Affairs Association specially telegraphed the central government yesterday, requesting that it consider the severity of the disaster in Hunan and list it as a special disaster area, and issue a large sum of relief money to save the survivors. The original text is as follows: Urgent, Chairman Xu Jun of the Nanjing Relief Affairs Committee, Hunan Province has been suffering from disasters, and misfortunes have followed one another. There is no year without warfare, droughts, and floods. This year, the banditry has not been quelled, and the floods have risen again. Since the beginning of summer, there has been continuous rain, which has not stopped until now. The disaster has spread throughout the province, and the misery is difficult to describe. The floods have continued to rise, and the disaster situation has expanded day by day. According to Xiangxiang, Xiangtan, Hengshan, Hengyang, Yueyang, Xiangyin, Changde, Taoyuan, Huarong, Nanxian, Yuanjiang, Anxiang, Hanshou, Chaling, Anren, Yiyang, Anhua, 溪 Guiyang, Xintian, Qiancheng, Yongsui, Yuanling, 淑Pu, Yongxing, Qiyang, Sangzhi, Shimen, Linli, Li County, Cili, Yizhang, Chen County, Pingjiang, Ningyuan, Yongshun, Dayong, Leiyang, Guzhang, Changsha, Huitong, and Huang County, and other forty-two counties. The urgent reports are filled with heavy disasters and are unbearable to read. Whether due to flash floods or waterlogging, the mountainous fields are filled with waves and have become泽国. The levee-protected fields have collapsed, and everything from homes to belongings has been washed away. Countless livestock and trees have been lost, and the number of deaths by drowning is estimated to be in the tens of thousands. The number of displaced people is also in the millions. Although the crops in the high-lying fields in other counties have not been flooded, they have also been affected by the prolonged rain, and 螟胜蟊贼, 暗长潜滋, damaged crops, and the harvest is hopeless. Moreover, the rain has not stopped, the flood is increasing day by day, and the insect pests are getting worse. Farmers have worked hard all year round, but they are now without hope. Survival is impossible, and the future is dire. If relief is not urgently sought, the old and weak will have no means of livelihood and will fill the ditches, and the young and strong will take risks, and they will inevitably become bandits, which is a pitiful phenomenon and a worrying hidden danger. Hunan Province has suffered many catastrophes, and its vitality is exhausted. The public and private sectors are in difficulty, and there is no way to raise relief funds. We can only sigh and look up at the roof, unable to fill the gap. In addition to the committee members conducting inspections in various ways, we implore you to consider the extraordinary disaster in Hunan and list it as a special disaster area. We urgently request that you appoint senior officials to come to Hunan for inspection, and issue a large sum of relief money to provide immediate relief. Upon further investigation, the Executive Yuan approved 100,000 yuan for emergency relief last year, but we have not received it despite repeated telegrams. We urge you to forward the letter to the Ministry of Finance and approve the full amount of emergency relief as soon as possible to save the disaster victims and eliminate hidden dangers. We eagerly await your orders, and we are grateful and impressed. Cao Bowen, Zhang Jiongcheng, and Xiwenganyin, Standing Committee Members of the Hunan Provincial Relief Affairs Association.

Canal Upstream Water Surge

Liang Guanying Requests Opening of the Zhaoguan Dam

The Great Flood of the Republic Era 10 [1921] Dared Not Lightly Open [the Dam]

A dispatch from Zhenjiang: In the past five days, the source of the Yi River in the upper reaches of the canal has changed from receding to a gradual surge. The Water Conservancy Bureau suddenly received a telegram from Director Mao from Gaoyou the day before yesterday (the 7th), reporting that the Yi River had surged more than ten feet, already showing an alarming trend. Today, telegrams were received continuously from various institutions and organizations of the Huaiyin County Government and Chamber of Commerce, stating that the water in the upper reaches of the canal was surging, and the first and second sluice gates of Huaiyin had been overflowed. The Yi River is arriving again, and the military and civilians are now cooperating to protect the dikes. Please quickly open the Zhaoguan Dam to release the upstream water. It has been more than eighty years since the Zhaoguan Dam was opened, and the diversion canal below the dam has also been quite silted up. During the great flood of the Republic Era 10 [1921], after much contention, it was ultimately not lightly opened. However, the Yi River is surging excessively, and the counties on the eastern bank of the upper reaches of the canal will inevitably become a land of swamps. The area near Mount Mailing is especially vast and boundless, and the mountain will be like an island in a lake or sea. Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Construction Department, and Pei, the Chief Engineer of the Water Conservancy Bureau, led engineering staff and carried large sums of construction funds to inspect the upper and lower reaches of the canal north of the river this afternoon. Furthermore, on the 7th, the water level at Yumatou rose by five minutes [of a foot], reaching a water depth of one foot eight inches nine minutes. Bengbu dropped nine centimeters, with a water depth of nineteen meters seventy-seven. Yaowan rose another nine inches six centimeters, reaching a water depth of twenty-two meters fifty-two.

A dispatch from Yangzhou: The Chief Commander of the Twenty-fifth Route telegraphed Supervisor Su yesterday, saying that the canal water was surging and had been reported repeatedly. Recently, due to the sudden arrival of the Yi River, it has become increasingly turbulent. The areas near Matouzhen are particularly critical. The first sluice gate is only two inches away [from overflowing], and the second sluice gate has already caused flooding. Although the officers and soldiers are blocking day and night, it is useless to block in the east and overflow in the west, and there is no comprehensive solution. The Shuangqiaodongkou of the third sluice gate has not yet been repaired. If it continues to rise, the dikes of the Huaichen sluice gates may collapse and become irreparable. The Zhaoguan Dam in Gaoyou can be opened in the event of large water according to precedent. If the dam is opened, the lives and property of the people in the counties north of the river will have a glimmer of hope. In addition to directly telegraphing Chairman Ye, this telegram is for your attention. However, it is still unknown how the person in charge will handle it.

Another dispatch: The water level in Jiangduzhou, discharged from the Chexin and Nan San dams, did not rise or fall on the 7th and 8th, which can be considered stable. The water level record at Gaoyou Yumatou fell to one foot eight inches seven minutes five on the 6th, and rose one inch again on the 7th, with a total water depth of one foot eight inches eight minutes five. However, the northwest wind has been strong in recent days, and the Shao embankment is still dangerous.陸士銓, the section chief of the county, together with the Jiangdu section of the public works office, surveyed and prepared to raise the embankment. The areas to be raised have been determined: Yangzi Bridge in Guazhou, Wantou near the city, and Wangzhuang and Lujin in Shaobo, all to be raised by three feet, with a top width of one zhang. The county is responsible for first building the five-foot (wide) section facing the water, with a deadline of one week for completion. Yesterday (the 7th), the county government, in accordance with provincial orders, ordered the recruitment of 1,500 civilian laborers within three days, carrying tools, to be used by the Water Conservancy Bureau, and provided them with food and wages. The Public Security Bureau was specially ordered to rush the recruitment. The bureau feared that the recruited laborers would misunderstand and suspect it was for military use, so it ordered Liao Chuliang, the chief inspector, to go to Shao early on the 8th with personnel from the Water Conservancy Bureau to recruit nearby along the embankment, designating the specific embankment to be rushed to build, so as to encourage enthusiastic recruitment. It is estimated that it can be completed in three or four days. It is also learned that Sun Hongzhe, Director of the Construction Department, will pass through Yangzhou from the province around 3 p.m. on the 8th to go to Gaoyou for work. The Shaobo public assistance temporary office for the embankment work telegraphed to the provincial and civil construction departments, saying that the wind is tight and the waves are beating the embankment, and the danger is imminent. The cost of rushing to repair is huge, and the strength is weak and unsustainable. Please order the county to allocate funds quickly to protect the embankment and save lives. Hundreds of millions of lives depend on this. Please telegraph a reply quickly.

Brief Regulations for the Issuance of Salt Tax Treasury Bills

Approved and Promulgated by the Ministry of Finance Yesterday

The Ministry of Finance issued 80 million yuan of short-term salt tax treasury bills of the Republic Era 20 [1931] and issued them on the 1st. The ministry formulated and promulgated 14 articles of the brief regulations for the issuance of the treasury bills yesterday. They are recorded as follows: (1) Total amount: Face value of 80 million yuan; (2) Types: Four types: 5,000 yuan, 1,000 yuan, 100 yuan, and 10 yuan; (3) Interest: Monthly interest of 8 li; (4) Issuance: These treasury bills are issued at 98% of the face value, that is, each 100 yuan face value actually receives 98 silver yuan; (5) Method of repayment of principal and interest: These treasury bills are repaid in 78 months. Starting from August of the Republic Era 20 [1931], repay 1% of the principal per month in the first year, 1.1% of the principal per month in the second year, 1.2% of the principal per month in the third year, 1.3% of the principal per month in the fourth year, 1.4% of the principal per month in the fifth year, 1.5% of the principal per month in the sixth year, 1.6% of the principal per month in the first to fifth months of the seventh year, and 2% of the principal per month from the sixth month until the end of January of the Republic Era 27 [1938]. Interest decreases with the principal; (6) Issuing agencies: Central, China, and Jiaotong banks in various places, and other designated sales agencies. When subscribers pay, the receiving bank will fill out a reservation coupon, indicating the amount, type, and number of coupons, and the amount of silver paid. When the official treasury bills are printed, a notice will be issued for exchange; (7) Fund: These treasury bills are designated to use the salt tax collected by the national treasury as the fund to pay the principal and interest. The full amount listed in the principal and interest repayment schedule is allocated each month; (8) Fund custody: The fund for these treasury bills is concurrently managed by the Fund Management Committee entrusted by the Ministry of Finance and Taxes, and the Central, China, and Jiaotong banks are designated for payment. All 5,000 yuan and 1,000 yuan types must have the original coupon presented by the coupon holder to the managing bank or managing office for verification, and the principal and interest coupons are cut off to receive the principal and interest. The 100 yuan and 10 yuan types will have the monthly principal and interest coupons cut off to receive the principal and interest; (10) Receipts and payments: All receipts and payments for these treasury bills are mainly in general silver yuan; (10)(1) Method of deducting principal and interest: According to Article 5, if a person subscribes to these treasury bills within August of the Republic Era 20 [1931], they will be given the first period's principal and interest coupon. If a person subscribes within September, the first period's principal and interest coupon should be cut off, and the cash payment should be deducted by the first period's principal for every 100 yuan. The same will be done for later periods, which should be noted on the reservation coupon or the receipt issued by the solicitation agency for separate issuance of coupons; (10)(2) Solicitation expenses: The handling fee for soliciting these treasury bills is set at 1%. Whether it is an individual or an agency, all those who solicit coupon funds and hand them over to the treasury can enjoy this benefit to show encouragement. However, if there are items such as discount exchange fees for remitting funds, they must not be developed separately; (10)(3) Deadline for payment: The solicitation agencies that solicit these treasury bills shall remit them once every five days and must not delay. Otherwise, the interest for the delay shall be borne by the solicitation agency; (10)(4) Receipt and payment report: Each bank shall list and report the coupon funds received and the principal and interest paid each month to the solicitation agency and the Ministry of Finance for verification. Each bank's paid principal and interest shall also be listed and reported monthly, and the paid principal and interest coupons shall be sent to the Fund Management Committee for collection and forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for verification and cancellation.

Local Dispatches

Fengxian

Inspection of Hymen of Female Actors in a Case of Abduction and Indecent Assault：In Hujiaqiao Town of this county, a troupe of male and female actors came to perform new dramas at a borrowed venue. Before even three days had passed, a young man named Xu Shouchang from Hangzhou, who had arrived from Shanghai, reported to the local public security station that Wei Guobin, a male actor in the troupe, had lured and indecently assaulted his younger sister, Xu Qingzhen (who was also an actress in the troupe). However, the station lacked evidence to prove whether the Xus were siblings. Therefore, they brought all involved to the county for investigation. At the same time, Xu Shouchang also submitted a certificate from an officer of the Fifth Division and filed a lawsuit. President Shen then appointed Prosecutor Xu Chengshen to open a court for interrogation. Xu Shouchang claimed that he lived in Zhabei, Shanghai, and worked in journalism. The girl was his third younger sister. She had been missing since the 15th of last month. After repeated investigations, he learned that Wei Guobin, who was involved in new dramas, had abducted her. Xu Qingzhen testified that she was fifteen years old and did not know Wei Guobin. On the night of the 15th of last month, she was cooling off in the Great World entertainment center when Wei, in collusion with an accomplice, lured her to a hotel and confined her, forbidding her from leaving. He then took her to Minhang by steamer and forced her to perform in new dramas. Since she was alone and helpless, she had no choice but to obey his orders and went with him to various places. She was indecently assaulted five times. Wei Guobin, on the other hand, claimed that the girl worked as a hostess at the rooftop garden of the Wing On Company in Shanghai and was a promiscuous woman. She had voluntarily joined the troupe and was paid wages every day. There was no indecent assault. Prosecutor Xu Chengshen, finding the testimonies of both parties contradictory and lacking proof, ordered that Wei Guobin be detained. As for whether Xu Qingzhen had been indecently assaulted, he had sent her to the county clinic's Western medical director, Hu Dacai, and female doctors Zhou Ruiyu and Wang Ziying for examination. The results showed that the girl's development was not complete, and her hymen had a crack but was not broken. However, there were semen secretions outside her labia minora, and the area was scarlet red, resembling inflammation. Based on this report, the county government had planned to continue the interrogation yesterday, but since the plaintiff, Xu Shouchang, had returned to Shanghai, the verdict will be announced next Friday.

Chuansha

Turmoil Over the Removal of a Principal: Chen Jiajie, the former director of the County Education Bureau, who also served as a member of the Party Rectification Committee, caused a student strike due to planting his cronies since he concurrently served as the director on May 1st of this year. The Education Department clearly ordered his dismissal. After the news of Chen's dismissal was announced, he dismissed the principals of Mingqiang and Minghua schools, which had achieved good results, and appointed his relatives and friends, causing a public outcry. Tao Qiqing, the new director, took over on the 1st of this month. After learning the truth, he was deeply afraid of causing disputes again, which would affect the progress of local education. He immediately collected opinions from education inspectors as the standard for the advancement and retreat of principals and convened a bureau affairs meeting on the morning of the 7th to discuss. As a result, Gu Zhiyong, the principal of Huibei Elementary School, was allowed to return to his post. The other dismissed principals were also reappointed or transferred. A turmoil has been calmed.

Sun Shoumei Sues After Release From Prison: Sun Xiangyun, a wealthy resident of Xinzhuang, was kidnapped two years ago. The bandits sent a letter demanding 120,000 yuan. The Sun family, Sun Xu Shi and her daughter Baozhen, suspected that their nephew Sun Shoumei was involved in the kidnapping. They filed a lawsuit and the Songjiang County Government, which also handled judicial affairs, detained him for investigation. The water police captured several bandits, including Huang Miaogen and Liu Asi. The County Court was established and the case was transferred to the court for re-investigation. The kidnappers, including Huang, did not involve Sun Shoumei. Apart from Huang Miaogen and Liu Asi, who were executed, Sun Shoumei was declared innocent. He was detained for one year and ten months. Sun's businesses, such as the Meiyuan Garden, completely withered, causing considerable losses. Both material and spiritual aspects were sacrificed. He sued Sun Xu Shi and her daughter for false accusations and perjury to the Procuratorate. The court opened an investigation yesterday. After the plaintiff stated the previous situation and the defendant testified, the prosecutor said that whether the false accusation was established in this case needed further study. Since several defendants in this case had appealed to the High Court, the original files would be returned after the trial. They were ordered to return.

Returning Home in the Same Car and Suddenly Suffering from a Poisonous Hand: Wu Baozhi from Jurong and his fellow villagers

Page 12

Ren Da, Huogen, Dashuigen, and Ni Sheng were all attendants in a bathhouse on Sanma Road in Shanghai. The four people then jointly paid a deposit of 700 yuan. After many days of arguing in Shanghai, the problem could not be resolved. On the evening of the 7th, the four people took the night train to Danyang to return to their hometown to seek a solution. Wuxi

Kidnapped Victim in Yixing Safely Escapes: Chen Xida and Chen Songda, villagers in Shengzhuang Village, Zhangzhu, Yixing, were kidnapped by a gang of bandits. Chen Songda had already been released. It is now learned that Chen Xida was also released from the bandit den the day before yesterday. The Chen family was extremely happy. After Xida returned home, he recounted the experience of being kidnapped, saying, "It has been twenty days since I was kidnapped by the bandits. In the bandit den, two or three bandits took turns guarding me every day and did not allow me to move freely. I had to move several times a day. When it came time to eat, I was taken to the top of the mountain, and there were no tables or stools. We all sat on the ground. After eating, I was still escorted to the bottom of the mountain and confined to the bandit den." Later, one of the bandit leaders talked to me. He said, "You have been kidnapped by our team for a long time. Our team has also sent a letter to notify your family, but no reply has been received and no one has come to negotiate. Now, our team has sent someone to Shen's family to investigate and found that your family is indeed without money, so we will release you today."

Crackdown on Private Counterfeit Coin Production Organization: Gao Chongshan, the director of the first public security bureau, reported yesterday that Pan Renbiao, a resident of No. 4 Tushuguan Road, near Guanqian Street, was privately producing counterfeit coins at home and mixing them on the market, causing a lot of harm. Please send the police to arrest them quickly. Director Gao, according to the report, immediately sent Bureau Officer Qin Jingqing, led Patrol Captain Wu Quan, and informants to execute it. After arriving at the destination, he ordered the informants to buy counterfeit coins with four silver dollars. Sure enough, he bought 22 yuan of lead counterfeit silver dollars. Bureau Officer Qin, with the real money in hand, immediately rushed in and arrested Pan Renbiao first, and found 26 counterfeit silver dollars, 8 counterfeit double dimes, 4 models, and half a can of powder. He then brought the witnesses to the bureau and sent them to the headquarters. After the third section staff Zhang Shuping opened the court and interrogated him, Pan Renbiao confessed that he used to work in a military band. After losing his job, he could not maintain his livelihood, so he did not deny privately producing counterfeit coins. Zhang Jun verified the confession and ordered the detention. Yesterday (9th), he prepared a document and sent it to the county court for interrogation according to law.

A Citywide Furor Over Catching Monkeys: Qin Xiaolu, the former county magistrate of this county, now raises two monkeys, male and female, in Xiaolou Lane in Wancheng. They are docile. At 4 p.m. the day before yesterday, one of the female monkeys escaped. After the Qin family noticed, it was gone. At about 8 o'clock in the evening, the monkey had sneaked into the nursery in front of the new temple and hugged a three-year-old baby and fled. The nanny saw it and immediately stepped forward to chase it before she threw the baby down. But the child was half dead. After a while, the baby went to Zhu Bingdie's house, next door to the nursery, and destroyed the furnishings in the room one by one. He then went to a hawker's house and ate large amounts of honey peaches and watermelon and other fresh fruits. Yesterday (9th) at 9 a.m., the monkey was running east and west on the roofs in and out of the north gate. So, merchants and residents came out to catch it, but the monkey was cunning, so it was not caught. Xu Jigui, the director of the Public Security Bureau, also heard the news. Fearing that it would disrupt public order, he sent four detectives with pistols to catch it. For a time, it spread throughout the city, and the viewers were like a wall. By 4 p.m., it was rumored that the monkey had been caught by detectives on the roof of a certain family.

The Silk Market is in Decline, Requesting Relief: The silk factories in this county and the Silk Factory Association jointly presented to the government, after failing in business last year, were approved to issue 8 million yuan of silk industry relief public bonds, and starting from May 20 this year, 30 yuan of public debt funds were collected per package from the customs when raw silk was exported. Since the beginning of the request for relief last year, it has been a year to date, and the factories have also been bearing the repayment of public debt funds for three months, but the so-called approved public bonds have not yet been issued. The factories are looking forward to it, waiting eagerly. And the government is handling this public bond, on the one hand, to relieve the silk factories that lost money in the 19th year of the Republic and encourage the export of raw silk. On the other hand, they also said that those who could not continue to start work this year would not be eligible to receive the public bonds. Therefore, although the capital of the factories was lost last year and they owed money to the money houses as much as 40,000, 50,000, 60,000, or 70,000, they had to borrow east and west, pledge items, and collect cash as little as several thousand and as much as 10,000 or 20,000 this year to start work with difficulty in order to obtain relief public bonds and repay the money owed to the money houses. This kind of quenching thirst with poison is really a great sigh. In addition, this year's spring and summer cocoons have been affected by the weather, and the harvest is poor, less than 20% compared to previous years. Now, the factories are short of raw materials. If it is an ordinary business, then rare things are expensive, and the price of silk will naturally skyrocket. However, the European and American silk markets are manipulated by Japanese merchants, so the downstream is becoming more and more depressed, and the sales of Chinese silk are extremely sluggish. At present, the price of silk is only 830-840 taels per load, which is not enough to offset the cost of cocoons. The remaining 200 taels of silk reeling is completely unavailable. The managers of the factories calculate on average that each factory reeling one load of silk a day has to lose more than 200 taels of silver. The managers of the factories are in this desperate situation, and they really want to cry without tears and want to die without being able to. The association has received letters from the managers of the factories and has carefully reviewed the current situation of the factories, believing that it is very dangerous. Yesterday, it specifically presented a document to the county government for review and asked them to quickly find ways to coordinate relief to maintain the silk industry.

The Impact of Building a Dam on the Sangan River in Changshu: Yangku Fushou Township in the Seventh District has a low terrain. This time, it suffered a heavy flood. The reason is that Changshu is on a higher elevation, and built a dam without authorization, causing the water to be discharged poorly. After the flood, a few landlords in Changshu, who did not understand the overall situation, not only destroyed the dam of the first Sangan River, but also dammed the second and third Sangan rivers at the same time. The farmers in the township gathered thousands of people the day before yesterday, intending to gather themselves to destroy the dam. The district chief, Wang Wenkui, said that the original purpose of dredging the Sangan River was to guide the water source and develop water conservancy, so that it would connect to the Yangtze River in the north and reach Taihu Lake in the south, which could be verified. He has persuaded them on the one hand to wait for the county government to review and handle it. He also presented to the county to quickly telegraph the Changshu County Government to order the dam to be demolished so as to unblock the water flow and send personnel to survey and devise relief measures to benefit people's livelihood. (According to farmers in the fourth district of Changshu, the farmers blocked the flow and built a dam in the Sangan River, causing the farmers in the fifth district to prevent it. The county sent personnel to demolish it, causing a trend. The farmers in the fourth district strive to If you want to demolish the Sangan River Dam, you must first dredge the Thirteen Weigang, which is difficult to solve.)

Organizations in Various Industries Hold a Meeting to Sever Economic Ties with Japan: The County Chamber of Commerce held a joint meeting of the executive and supervisory committees and a general meeting of various industries on the afternoon of the 8th to discuss measures to sever economic ties with Japan: (1) Formulate an organizational outline, nominate the directors of the various departments, Director of General Affairs: Wu Shuying, Investigation: Deng Yu, Registration: Zhang Jianmen, Evaluation: Shen Danqing; (2) Notify all industries to immediately stop purchasing Japanese goods. The Japanese goods in stock in various industries must be registered with the association within one week and inspected immediately; (3) Raise funds and send them to rescue overseas Chinese. Send a telegram to the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Aid Overseas Chinese Association to strictly inspect Japanese goods to cut off the source.

Residents of North Gate Petition the County Government: The riverbank outlets and Touzhaikou in this county experienced several incidents yesterday morning (the 5th), but were successfully contained. Unexpectedly, at around 5 PM yesterday, leaks reappeared at the riverbank outlet and Touzhaikou, and by 9 PM, they were still not blocked. Residents outside the North City were greatly alarmed, fearing water would enter the city. They gathered two to three thousand people and went to the county government to petition for: (1) efforts to contain the leaks at Touzhaikou and the riverbank outlet; (2) no accumulation of soil at the four city gates; and (3) the county magistrate to hand over those who privately opened the dams. County Magistrate Wang responded that he would of course make every effort to contain the leaks at Touzhaikou and the riverbank outlet. Regarding the second point, local elders said that soil should be accumulated at the four city gates during major floods, and asked everyone not to misunderstand. While he was speaking, a gong was sounded again at the riverbank outlet to report to the county that the leaks were still not contained. County Magistrate Wang immediately rushed to supervise the containment work, and both leaks were blocked late into the night.

Hangzhou

Qianjiang Ferry Transferred to Private Management: The Qianjiang River is a crucial transportation route between eastern and western Zhejiang. Since the establishment of the public ferry during the Qing Dynasty, it has been convenient for travelers. Recently, although cement docks have been built on both banks, the official management has suffered from fixed funding, leading to the gradual damage and reduction of ferries and boats due to years of neglect. Passengers often complain. To improve the situation, Shi Ying, the Construction Department Director, first allocated funds to repair ships and then recruited forty gentlemen from Shanghai and Hangzhou, including Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xuanchu, Wang Zhuzhai, and Wang Xiangquan, to form the Qianjiang Ferry Committee. The plan is to transfer the affairs of the Ferry Bureau to the Committee for management, with a monthly allocation of 4,000 yuan. Any shortfall will be raised by the Committee. It is reported that the provincial government has already decided to invite the committee members to a luncheon soon to discuss the handover and management matters.

Accident on the Xiaoshao Section of the Hangzhou-Shaoxing Highway: A passenger vehicle, No. 51, on the Xiaoshao section of the Hangshao Highway, departed from Wuyunmen at 10 AM the day before yesterday. Near Qianqing, an elderly woman was walking along the road, and the driver, unable to avoid her in time, caused the vehicle to overturn. Nine passengers were injured, the most seriously injured being Ding Zhimei, the manager of the Yutai Rice Shop in Shaoxing, and the driver Zhao Fengshui. The injured were taken to the Xiaoshan Jimin Hospital for treatment by ambulance. According to the doctor's diagnosis, Ding's shoulder blade was broken, and he had a back wound of about six inches. After an emergency injection of a cardiac stimulant, his life was no longer in danger.

Investigation of Education Funds in Various Counties and Cities of Guangdong Province

Guangzhou City Accounts for Over 1.3 Million Yuan

There are a total of ninety-four counties and three cities in Guangdong Province. An investigation has found that eighty-six counties and cities have established Education Bureaus. Among them, Guangzhou City has the highest education expenditure, accounting for over 1.3 million yuan annually. Below this, education funds are limited, which is largely the reason for the underdeveloped local education. Difficulty in Selecting a Director for the Zhejiang Provincial Library

Yang Licheng, the director of the Zhejiang Provincial Library, was dismissed after serving for three years due to poor management. The Education Department then appointed Zhao Mian, the director of the Third Section, to take over. However, Zhao declined, believing that the library would be difficult to reorganize. The Education Department then appointed Ma Zongrong as the successor, but it is feared that Ma will also find it difficult to take office.

Compulsory Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province

Joint Office Requests Enrollment of Students

The Shanghai County Education Bureau received a letter yesterday from the Joint Office for the Preparation of Compulsory Education in Various Counties of Jiangsu Province, stating: "It has been found that the office, in order to promote compulsory education, urgently needs to train teachers. A request was submitted to the Ministry of Education for approval to continue running the correspondence department for teacher training. The regulations and the application forms to be filled in during registration have been enclosed, and we hereby request that you widely disseminate this information and designate teachers to participate in the training. Now that the third session of students is enrolling, the office strives for universality to increase efficiency. Therefore, we have formulated enrollment measures and request that your bureau refer to them and implement them: (1) In addition to teachers from various locations voluntarily participating in the training, please also ask the Education Bureau of each county to examine the teachers' levels, determine the quota for each school district, and temporarily assign a number of people to register for participation, so that the supply can better meet the needs. (2) Elementary schools with four or more classrooms should immediately recommend one teacher to participate in research as an incentive for further study. (3) Single-level elementary school principals will be paid by the Education Bureau (12 yuan per school) to participate in the research together, in order to improve educational efficiency. (4) Unqualified elementary school teachers should participate in the training in accordance with the Central University's Order No. 9, otherwise their teaching positions will be terminated. (5) Private school teachers who can be improved should be ordered to participate in the training. (6) The Education Bureau should order several copies for reference in educational guidance. (7) It is best if the Education Bureau subsidizes half of the training fee for participating students (6 yuan per person). The training fee paid by the bureau can be withdrawn from the compulsory education mu tax or the teacher reward fund from the tin foil tax, in accordance with the approved plan."

Education Circle in Wuxian County

Expressing Dissatisfaction with Director Wu

The principals of the county-run elementary schools in Wuxian County are alarmed by the Education Bureau's announcement of austerity policies and improper measures. This situation has been brewing until now without a solution. Today, 174 principals have presented the facts and unanimously demanded Wu's removal. They have issued a declaration calling for assistance from all sectors and sent telegrams to the Provincial Government, the Ministry of Education, the Education Department, the County Government, and the County Party Consolidation Committee, requesting rectification. The original telegram is as follows (omitted titles): "We, the undersigned, have investigated that since the establishment of education in Wuxian County in the 29th year of Guangxu in the Qing Dynasty, nearly 30 years have passed. The standard of treatment for elementary school teachers has not been improved, while the cost of living has increased tenfold or more. Maintaining a livelihood is precarious. Now, Wu Yaozhang, the director of the Wuxian County Education Bureau, disregards the actual situation and repeatedly reduces education funding. All the measures are also improper. We hereby present the details to Your Excellency: (1) It is impossible to reduce funding. The daily increase in the cost of living and the meager treatment of teachers have been described above. Recently, the National Assembly and the Ministry of Education have repeatedly instructed that the treatment of elementary school teachers should be appropriately increased based on local conditions. However, the director ignores this. The solemn orders of the Ministry are treated as mere formalities. Even if it is said that funding is insufficient and measures must be taken to make up for it, the most urgent task is to improve revenue. However, this is not taken into consideration. Moreover, in recent years, the increase in the bureau's internal expenses is astonishing. Before 1924, the annual bureau expenses were only about 2,000 yuan. Now, it has reached over 30,000 yuan. Is this reasonable? (2) The administrative measures are improper. A. The re-division of school districts is baseless. This time, the eight school districts have been changed to six school districts, which is not based on autonomous regions or public security regions. Instead, the existing school districts have been arbitrarily divided and merged without careful consideration. This lacks caution. B. Elementary school principals should be appointed for a long term, as stated in the Provisional Constitution, in order to encourage dedicated service and improve educational efficiency. Since Principal Jiang Yongyuan took over Pingzhi Elementary School, he established senior grades and reorganized the school into a complete elementary school. The students have flourished, making the school the best in the county. The results are remarkable and widely recognized. However, regardless of his interests, he is transferred elsewhere, and his successor is arbitrarily appointed. Principal Wei Yongyao of Weiting Elementary School and Principal Yan Jiajin of Mudu Elementary School have achieved remarkable results since taking office, and the students have also made daily progress. Now, they are being reorganized into central elementary schools and placing eliminated education committee members. They claim to respect the principals' expertise and appoint them as specialist instructors, but this was neither agreed upon beforehand nor is the title of instructor retained afterwards. As leaders, they treat their work as child's play. Such reversed measures make every principal feel insecure. (3) Disregard for Party discipline. Holding commemorative weeks has long been ordered by the Central Committee. However, the bureau sometimes does not hold them, and the county party headquarters has also heard of this and urged attention. Furthermore, the Central Committee recently ordered that when hiring staff, the Party headquarters should be given priority. When dismissing staff, non-Party members should be given priority. However, the director is the opposite. For example, the principals of Pingzhi and Weiting are all Party members, but they are deliberately transferred away from the schools. Most of the bureau's staff are non-Party members. From this one aspect, it can be seen that his behavior is contrary to the principles and infuriating. In summary, we have listed the facts and respectfully request Your Excellency to review and quickly rectify the situation. We await your orders with utmost urgency. [Signed] Wang Jia and 174 other principals of Ban Huan Elementary School."

This year's Summer Mandarin Promotion Meeting is held in Shanghai. The main points of this Mandarin Promotion Meeting are three: (1) to promote the relationship between Mandarin and the Three Principles of the People; (2) the necessity of the Association convening a national Mandarin education discussion meeting; (3) the reasons for the Association's expanding its organization and broadly gathering comrades; (6) Jin ChengZhang sang the phonetic symbol song; (7) Li WeiYue reported: (1) The Association has publicly recommended cadre Qi TieHen to Japan and Guo HouJue to Southeast Asia to promote the national sincerity; (2) The Association's 20th year membership recruitment team, in Nanjing, has set up five teams, three of which have been established. Ninth Annual Anglo-American Women's Tennis Tournament

America Wins Wightman Cup 5-2

America wins five singles matches | Britain wins two doubles matches

| Tennis Queen Mrs. Moody Defies All |

Frais Mountain, 8th - The American women today reclaimed the Wightman Cup from the British women. This annual event, now in its ninth year, was won by Britain at Wimbledon last year. Of these nine tournaments, America has won five times and Britain four.

| Total of Seven Matches |

A total of seven matches were played: five singles and two doubles. America won all three singles matches yesterday and won two more today. The final two doubles victories went to Britain. The complete results are listed below:

(1) Mrs. Moody (USA) 6-1 6-4 Mlle. Moffatt (GB)

(2) Helen Jacobs (USA) 8-6 6-4 Miss Nuthall (GB)

(3) Mrs. Harper (USA) 6-3 4-6 9-7 Miss Round (GB)

(4) Helen Jacobs (USA) 6-4 6-2 Mlle. Moffatt (GB)

(5) Mrs. Moody (USA) 6-4 6-2 Miss Nuthall (GB)

(6) Mrs. Sheba-Baron and Mlle. Moffatt (GB) 6-4 10-8 Mrs. Wightman and Miss Van Frale (USA)

(7) Miss Nuthall and Mrs. Gettings-Islands (GB) 8-6 5-7 6-3 Mrs. Moody and Mrs. Harper (USA)

| First Day Singles |

America Wins Three Straight

Helen Wins Two Sets - American Helen Wills Moody and British Miss Phyllis Moffatt began their battle. Helen's powerful serve and superb smash left her opponent helpless. She won the first set 6-1. In the second set, Moffatt counterattacked strongly, but ultimately fell short and was defeated. Helen won again 6-4.

Jacobs Wins After Losing - American Miss Helen Jacobs defeated British Miss Nuthall 8-6, 6-4. In the first set, Jacobs lost the first four games and the situation was precarious. Unexpectedly, Jacobs relied on her calm approach to tie the score at 5-5, and then won 8-6. In the second set, Miss Nuthall, affected by the hot sun, lost her form and Jacobs won 6-4.

Harper Wins Hard-Fought Victory - Of the three matches that day, the most intense and memorable was the match between Mrs. Harper and Miss Dorothy Round. Mrs. Harper won the first set 6-3. Miss Round won the second set 6-4. The third set lasted sixteen games. Mrs. Harper fought hard against her strong opponent and finally won 9-7, taking the final victory 2-1.

| Second Day Singles |

America Wins Again

Helen Jacobs Wins Again - On the 8th, in singles, American Helen Jacobs faced British Moffatt. Initially, Moffatt’s powerful smash return of Helen’s chop was well-received by the audience. Moffatt took the lead 4-2 in the first set, and America seemed about to suffer a setback, but Helen quickly tied the score at 4-4, stepped up the pace, and won the first set 6-4. In the complete contrast between smash and chop in the first set, Helen won easily 6-2.

Mrs. Moody Shows Her Power - In the fifth singles match, American Wills Moody faced British Nuthall. At first, Nuthall made Mrs. Moody run all over the court, but in the end, she could not maintain her lead, made repeated mistakes, and committed major serving errors. The scores for the two sets were 6-4, 6-2.

| Final Two Doubles |

British Team Wins

In the final two doubles matches, the British team emerged victorious. Mrs. Sheba-Baron and Mlle. Moffatt defeated American Mrs. Wightman and Miss Pan Furly, 6-4, 10-8. The second match was very intense. In the last doubles match, the British first team, Miss Nuthall and Mrs. Extinguished Island, defeated the American first team, Mrs. Moody and Mrs. Harper. The first and second sets were close, with scores of 8-6, 5-7, 6-6.
