Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday that the weather in the lower reaches of the Yangtze River is sultry and humid, with showers. A hurricane will pass between Naba and Ishigaki Island, and may turn northwest. The weather in the entire eastern part and north of Taiwan Bay is bad. The center of the hurricane is currently threatening the local coast and may enter the Zhoushan Islands and the mouth of the Yangtze River. Also, the highest temperature in the local area in the 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday was 90.7 and the lowest was 78. On the same day last year, the highest was 94.5 and the lowest was 74.1.

Letter

Dear Editor, I read a news item in the Local News column of today's newspaper entitled "Public Bus in Shanghai South Causes Accident." The facts are not consistent with the actual situation. At 9:15 a.m. yesterday, a downbound public bus No. 19 of Route 3 of our company, driven by driver Wu Xiukun, arrived at the Xin Xiaodongmen bus stop. When passengers were about to get off, a armored silver transport vehicle of the China Reclamation and Banking Corporation drove out diagonally from the left rear, intending to cross our company's vehicle. Seeing the front vehicle driving, they panicked and the rear right wheel of the vehicle rubbed against the left front wheel and wing plate of our company's vehicle. The silver transport vehicle was also equipped with armor, which was heavy on top and light on the bottom, and overturned into the tram track. The local French police and the nearest smoke shop eyewitnessed and proved that the silver transport driver was driving illegally. The French police station's vehicle office sent the No. 41 French police chief to the scene of the accident, used a tape measure to measure the road surface, and surveyed the road according to the road traffic regulations. After reporting to the Xiaodongmen French police station for preliminary questioning, it was also designated that the fault lay with the other party. The responsibility for the accident should be fully borne by the driver of the Reclamation and Banking Corporation. In addition to estimating the repair costs of the damaged wings and the loss of business interruption, a list was prepared and a request for compensation from the other party will be submitted at 9 a.m. tomorrow (i.e., Monday) at the French police station's general vehicle office. It is hereby sent a letter requesting your newspaper to promptly correct the situation and avoid confusion. This is sincerely felt. To the Editor-in-Chief (Local News Column Editorial Department) of Shen Bao, Shanghai South Public Bus Company, August 9.

To the sender,

Proposed Request for Expedited Establishment of Automobile Factories and Self-Manufacturing of Tires, and Adoption of Gasoline Consultation Letter

Proposer Gu Zaizhen

Since the Road Association advocated road construction for more than ten years, the call for road construction has spread throughout the country. According to recent surveys, the roads completed in various provinces have exceeded 110,000 miles. The association's advocacy deserves admiration. However, as roads increase year by year, transportation also becomes more convenient. In the past, land transportation involved sedan chairs, small carts, donkey carts, and northern large carts. Now, these various vehicles have become outdated. Therefore, current transportation includes rickshaws, horse-drawn carriages, bicycles, automobiles, and trams. Among these, automobiles are the most convenient and fastest. As a result, rickshaws and horse-drawn carriages have been affected. Moreover, the roads built in various provinces recently, some of which are called automobile roads, and the asphalt expressways in major cities, are restricted to automobile traffic to prevent damage to the road surface. This indirectly promotes automobiles. As humans become more civilized and materials evolve, this is a natural trend. In recent times, social morals have declined, and people have become more extravagant. From high-ranking officials and wealthy merchants to vendors and laborers, they all take pride in riding in automobiles but are ashamed of not being able to manufacture them themselves. As a result, building one more road in the country is like selling a few more cars for foreigners. It is heartbreaking to say. Currently, foreign automobiles are sold in China, not only in major commercial ports such as Shanghai, Tianjin, Guangzhou, Xiamen, Hong Kong, Hankou, and provincial capitals, but also in remote areas where roads are accessible. Taking the capital city as an example, there are already more than 1,100 automobiles. If we count the automobiles in the whole country, there should be at least 100,000. In addition, tires, gasoline, and accessories are all imported. Even the tires manufactured by overseas Chinese merchants must come from the Dutch East Indies. According to a recent survey, the import report of the Jianghai Customs last year shows that the value of automobiles, gasoline, and accessories imported from foreign countries is about 20 million yuan. This only refers to Shanghai. The goods imported through the customs of Guangdong, Fujian, and Tianjin are not included. The amount of money exported annually in the whole country is staggering. If we do not catch up quickly and establish factories for self-manufacturing, not only will our economic rights be lost, but also if national defense becomes urgent, the sources of automobiles, gasoline, and tires will be cut off. There may be cars without tires, or tires without gasoline. The transportation of soldiers and food will be hampered, and this alone would be enough to lead to the downfall of the country. Automobiles are vehicles for transporting goods in peacetime, but they can also be converted into armored vehicles for carrying cannons in wartime. Therefore, if automobiles can be self-manufactured, their sizes and styles can be specified, and armor and load-bearing capacity can be planned in advance. This way, the cars sold in peacetime can be used as armored vehicles in wartime. With prior planning and preparation, we will not be caught unprepared in times of war. Moreover, in the face of many soldiers and bandits, it is impossible to reduce the number of soldiers, and it is also impossible to eliminate the bandits. Borrowing money and consuming funds to support this source of chaos, why not transform soldiers into workers and build automobile factories, turning non-production into production? With more factories, there will be fewer vagrants, and how can they be driven to take risks and become soldiers and bandits? Therefore, the construction of automobile factories cannot be delayed. The first thing to do when building a factory is to raise huge sums of money. At a time when the country is facing frequent troubles, it is not easy to talk about raising money. Whether it is issuing public bonds, attracting corporate stocks, or investing by Chinese merchants, if the government does not encourage and promote it, I am afraid there will never be a day of success. I believe that at the beginning of the trial operation of the automobile factory, it can be temporarily attached to the existing ordnance factories in various places. The scale should be small. After the products have achieved some success, it can be expanded so that the expenses will not be wasted and can achieve twice the result with half the effort. Moreover, the current ordnance factories in various places, such as Shanghai, Hanyang, Dezhou, Guangzhou, Gongxian, and Liaoyang, are large in scale, well-equipped, and have relatively abundant talent. Design, drawing, and manufacturing can be mutually used. If there are parts that cannot be self-manufactured, foreign engineers can be hired to manufacture them, and graduates of mechanical engineering from home and abroad can be recruited, or experienced craftsmen and clerks in the factory can be trained to work and taught other manufacturing and driving skills in their spare time. After the automobile parts can be completely self-manufactured, then the foreign engineers can be dismissed. As for the materials for car manufacturing, if China has its own products, all domestic products should be used to prevent the loss of economic rights and unemployment. Enriching the country and strengthening the people should be based on this. However, the cost of cars initially manufactured in China may be higher, resulting in few buyers. Even if there are durable, beautiful, and durable cars, I am afraid no one will care. However, if the government can handle it properly, there will be no shortage of cars without sales. At the beginning of the sale of Chinese-made cars, they should be sold at cost price and provide convenience for those who speak to order and transport. Preferential treatment should be given for paying taxes and obtaining licenses. On the one hand, the government should order its subordinate agencies to purchase and use them uniformly. In this way, Chinese cars will sell themselves without being sold. On the other hand, merchants should be encouraged to set up factories to imitate. With more factories and better products, strive for perfection. I think that in a few years, Chinese cars will not be difficult to surpass those in Europe and America.

The operation of automobiles depends entirely on tires. The raw materials for tire manufacturing depend on rubber. The tires manufactured by the Chen Jiageng Company of our country's overseas Chinese merchants include automobile tires, rickshaw tires, and bicycle tires. The quality is excellent, and the sales are wide. However, the tires manufactured by overseas Chinese merchants still need to come from the Dutch East Indies. It is very convenient to import them to our country in peacetime, but if diplomatic relations are severed, the impact on transportation will be significant. Moreover, rubber raw materials are not produced domestically. Fujian and Guangdong in our country are close to the tropics and should try to plant them. On the one hand, the government should establish rubber experiment stations to study cultivation, seed selection, and glue making. On the other hand, overseas Chinese should be encouraged to set up factories in the mainland to manufacture them themselves. It is not too late to prepare for a rainy day.

Gasoline is refined from petroleum. In the central part of Sichuan, the Shandan and Jiuquan of Gansu, the Dihua, Turpan, Yanqi of Xinjiang, the Yanken and Fushi in the northern part of Shaanxi, and the Zhenba County in the southern part of Shaanxi, petroleum springs out everywhere and is rich in storage. Moreover, the petroleum in Shaanxi was once deeply excavated, but it was interrupted because it was not completely penetrated and the oil quality did not spring up, and transportation was inconvenient. It is a pity. In recent years, the sales of gasoline, kerosene, and lubricating oil have become more and more extensive. In Shanghai alone, the amount of the above three types of oil imported last year exceeded 20 million gallons. If we count the amount of oil imported in the whole country, it is more than this number. At this time of petroleum , our country has no oil production. The price of oil is entirely manipulated by foreigners. Once the oil price increases sharply and foreign goods do not come, our country has no oil that can be used as a substitute for petroleum. Although it is expensive, it must be purchased and used. Losing power and harming profits, nothing is more serious than this. We should take this time to find ways to explore and refine them, especially in the oil-producing areas, and open up more roads so that the oil produced in the oil-producing areas can be transported to all parts of the country.

The above points are all urgent matters at present, and they are closely related to the promotion of road construction. If they can be implemented, the benefits of building a road can be reaped. The country is fortunate, and the society is fortunate. Is it appropriate? I respectfully await your decision.

World Briefs

— Seafarer

The Peculiar Habit of Buying Old Prisons

Buying land and houses is the most reliable way to make money in modern times. Of course, everyone likes it. However, the most interesting thing is that Mr. Thomas Oakley, a wealthy man from Luton, England, has the peculiar habit of buying abandoned old prisons. Previously, he had already bought prisons in Gosport, Derby, and Worcester. Recently, he spent £4,150 to buy Knutsford Jail in Cheshire. He plans to make the most of it and turn it into a hostel for coachmen. The price is extremely low. Each person only needs to pay three shillings a day to sleep and bathe, and breakfast is included. All the prison cells have been completely converted into bedrooms with 300 good beds. It can accommodate 300 people every night. There is a cement-paved open space of three acres in the prison, which can be used by coachmen to park empty cars. Three or four hundred cars can be accommodated. The prison has a total base of five acres and is located on the main road from London to Liverpool and Manchester. It is very suitable to be converted into a hostel for coachmen.

In addition to liking to buy old prisons, Mr. Wu has also bought a light cruiser, four airfields, a ditch in the Crystal Palace, part of the Grenagh Ammunition Factory, six or seven wineries, several cotton mills, and fourteen country mansions. This gentleman is truly a strange person.

Xu Shiying's Tragic Report

— Sun Choucheng

Since the beginning of summer this year, it has been raining continuously, and mountain floods have broken out. The size of the disaster area is unprecedented. The 62nd issue of this newspaper's pictorial weekly has published photos of floods in various places, and has also written a series of flood reviews every day to promote them. Leaders from all walks of life in this port recently launched the Shanghai Fundraising Association for Disaster Relief in Various Provinces. On the afternoon of the 6th, Xu Shiying reported on the disaster situation in various provinces during a discussion on fundraising methods at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. He beat his chest and stamped his feet, and shouted loudly, saying that there were already 16 provinces in the disaster area, with a population of more than 50 million. I am from Anhui. According to reports from my hometown, more than a dozen counties along the Huai River, such as Tianchang, Wuhe, Fuyang, and Mengcheng, are either located in low-lying areas and prone to flooding, or mountain floods have broken out and embankments have collapsed. Crops and livestock were destroyed, and the old and young were drowned. In Huoqiu, more than 8,000 people drowned in one day. In Fuyang County alone, more than 50,000 households were submerged. Guangjiwei in Anqing and Taoxingwei in Xuancheng are the most productive rice areas. Now they have also collapsed. Taihe, Qiupu, and Quanjiao counties have all become swamps. Other provinces such as Hunan, Henan, Jiangxi, Jiangsu, Hubei, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Guangdong have all suffered from floods. Taking the recent capital as an example, when I went to Beijing the other day, I passed Yaohuamen and saw groups of disaster victims gathered on the higher ground on both sides of the railway. The tragic situation was heartbreaking to see. Recently, there has been a focus on nationalism, and all 400 million people are called compatriots. I hope that you will regard the disaster-stricken compatriots as your own fathers, brothers, sons, sisters, and aunts, and donate generously to help them, which will bring endless blessings. The listeners were all moved.

A Glimpse of Japanese Propaganda

— Ming

Since the Wanbaoshan incident, the Japanese have been extensively disseminating information, and everyone knows it. Recently, the Japanese Consulate in this port has been sending wireless telegraphs to Fuzhou, Hankou, Beiping, and other places more than ten times a day. Each time, it must contain more than a hundred words, and they are all secret words composed of Roman characters, so it is difficult to understand their meaning. The registration number for each telegram is Riyoji. This is the exclusive registration number of the Japanese Consulate. According to a gentleman at the wireless telegraph station, this earns them no less than 100 gold every day. However, the Japanese are treacherous and wish that the people of the country would pay attention to it.

Anecdotes about the Zhu Jing Child Murder Case

— Cailiang

A guest from Jinshan once told me in detail about the recent child murder case that occurred in that place. I have selected those that have not been disclosed by various newspapers and recorded them for readers.

Rampant Debauchery The main protagonist in this case, Wang Tao, was originally a concubine who had been abandoned by a certain surname in Pinghu. Although she is old, her charm has not diminished. At first, she had an affair with Wang Yutian, the accountant of the house, and they were extremely intimate. Everything that Yutian enjoyed, no matter how expensive, she would not hesitate. They lived together like husband and wife. Then, after a long time, their love faded, and they often quarreled. Just then, a plasterer named Xia Aqing came to her house. He worked diligently, and his appearance was far better than Wang Yutian's, so he gained Wang Tao's trust. Gradually, a love triangle formed. Soon, her son Diqing's reputation spread far and wide, and he was very angry. He wanted to get rid of Xia and Wang quickly. Unexpectedly, the secret was not kept, and his mother heard about it. So, she summoned him to kill him. As the saying goes, "Adultery leads to murder." This incident proves it.

Running Away Due to Lost Love Since Diqing's murder was instigated by his mother, Xia Aqing and Xiaomama and others were all accomplices in the case. As for Yutian, although he was not at the scene, it is difficult to escape the suspicion of being an accomplice. Therefore, Yutian packed his bags and fled the day after the incident, and there has been no news of him so far. Even his family does not know where he lives. Now, in order to clarify the truth, the official authorities have stepped up their efforts to arrest him. I think the detectives are out looking for him, and there will be a day when the truth comes out.

Confession in Prison Wang Tao has been imprisoned and has suffered a lot. Whenever someone asks her about the past, she sheds tears. One day, a maid from her family came to visit her in prison. She suddenly looked pitiful and cried, "I really didn't want to kill my son. I was forced by the environment. I know I'm guilty, but I still want to ask Shao Nian Nai (her daughter-in-law) to forgive me." The maid heard this and agreed. From this, we know that Mencius's theory of the goodness of human nature is not without basis. But it is too late to regret it now that her conscience has been discovered.

Interesting Stories about the Play Since this case came out, people have been talking about it. The theaters in various places, which are good at speculation, have also regarded it as good material for playwriting. The Jin Yi Public Education Center recently rehearsed this play. The local scenery is particularly interesting. When the play was performed to the point where Wang Tao and others strangled Wang Diqing with a belt, a young woman suddenly made a strange sound and pointed and scolded the people in the play. At that time, the audience was puzzled and the whole hall was in an uproar. After inquiry, it was found that the woman was Diqing's widow. She was saddened by the scene and her eyebrows stood on end. The depth of the drama's ability to move people can be seen from this. Soon, the authorities ordered the play to be stopped because it was feared that it would cause trouble.

Newspapers Exclusively for Children to Read

— Sheng Han

In China, there are already many books and magazines published exclusively for children to read. However, there are hardly any newspapers exclusively for children to read.

The importance of current affairs education has been recognized by educators in general. However, most ordinary newspapers are written in classical Chinese, and the content is very difficult to understand. It is really not suitable for guiding children to study current affairs. And there are no newspapers exclusively for children to read, so educators in general regard it as a pity.

On June 1st last year, education colleagues from various places jointly created a "Children's Times." Their purpose is to "cultivate children's reading habits, enrich children's common sense, increase children's reading ability, encourage children's creative interest, and promote children's education." The newspaper is published every three days. It has now been published to issue 144. A small newspaper has sold to more than 20 provinces, and many schools in Japan, Annam, and Nanyang have subscribed to it. It is indeed China's only children's newspaper, and it is praised by many children's educators and children's writers. For example, Mr. Chen Heqin said, "The Children's Times can be said to be a unique work in China's recent publishing industry. It is worthy of attention by today's educators. There are many children's publications published in China now, but there are not many newspapers exclusively for children to read." Mr. Zhao Jingshen said, "The Children's Times" is very well edited. It is short and concise, so that children can acquire international news knowledge in the shortest time. It is indeed the first children's newspaper in modern times." Mr. Feng Zikai said, "The Children's Times. All the children in my family love to read it very much. Every time a new issue is obtained, they gather to watch it, as if they have obtained a treasure."

The editing style and printing format of the newspaper are very novel. The content is divided into three parts: "current affairs," "common sense," and "literature and art." The description of current affairs focuses on storytelling and systematization. The "Q&A" column is specially set up for common sense. Children can write to ask for answers if they have any difficult questions. The "Children's Garden" column is specially set up for literature and art to publish children's works. The text is entirely in vernacular Chinese, which is suitable for the level of students in the middle and high grades of elementary school. Regardless of text or pictures, the material is based on being interesting in principle, which is very suitable for children's psychology.

They are seeking convenience for education and happiness for children, and are not of a business nature, so the newspaper fee is very low. This is indeed a treasure for children.

It is written by members of the Bailian Literary Society. It has been published since issue 32. Memories of Escaping the Summer Heat in West Lake (3)

— Yuan Rongfang

Among the caves in the mountains, Yanhua Scenic Area is the most secluded and famous, and the road is the farthest. Shiwu and Ziyun are second, and Xixia is next. Only the coolness is suitable for summer, and the ancient Yanhua, the open Shiwu, the stone color of Ziyun, and the sound of the wind of Xixia make people unforgettable. In summer, when I encounter extreme heat, I often bring the Nanhua Sutra or several volumes of ancient poems and a small amount of dry food in the early morning for a day trip. Spreading out the scrolls on the stone table, the cold interest lasts forever. I don't know how high the temperature is outside the cave.

The Xiling Seal Society is the most beautiful place in the lake. The structure is exquisite, and the layout is simple. The slopes are high and low, and the wonderful scenery is layered. The bamboo path and thatched steps are full of ancient charm. The top of the mountain is hotter, so it is suitable to go there in the late evening. I often wait until the sun sets in the west and climb the Sizhao Pavilion to cool off. Spreading my clothes in the wind, I can see the whole lake. The clouds and trees are vast, and the shadows of the towers and mountains are all gone. The mist is vast, and the sound of the bells and people's voices are clear. This scenery and this joy cannot be obtained again.

People say that the spring lake is not as good as the autumn lake, and the autumn lake is not as good as the winter lake. I say that the sunny lake is not as good as the rainy lake, and the rainy lake is not as good as the moonlit lake. However, you cannot swim in the moonlit lake in winter, and it is not suitable in spring and autumn. Only summer is the best. Because the summer lake is hot and sultry, you must swim at night. You must have a moon at night to have fun. Therefore, every year in May, June, and July, after the first quarter of the moon, Hangzhou people compete for night swimming. For a time, luxurious boats are launched together, and brocade strings are played in a mixed way. There is a scene of the Southern Song Dynasty. I also often make appointments with two or three close friends to release the light in the middle of the stream. The bright moon hangs like a pearl, and the stars are scattered like chess pieces. The lake is wide and the sky is wide, and the storm is clear and the dew is cold. I suddenly feel tired and lose the heat, and the waves are crystal clear and the moon is broken into fish scales, as if sitting in an ice pot and swimming in a jade mirror. In this body, I am in the Guanghan Immortal Mansion. Or lean on the boat and blow the flute, learning from Su Shi's trip to the Red Cliff, or spread my clothes and hold the cup, looking for Li Bai's joy in Danyang, exploring the moon shadow in Santan, and visiting Xiaoqing at the foot of the mountain. Strolling leisurely on the Su Causeway, the weeping willows are reflected upside down. Staying in the lake pavilion, the carved platform is immersed. Looking at the surrounding green mountains from a distance, they are like flowers in the fog. And three or five fireflies flicker on the water surface, making shooting stars fly. Every time I wait for the bell of Nanping to move, I discuss making a return plan. Then the moon has set and the stars are horizontal, the fog is wet and the kudzu clothes are cool and refreshing to the skin. I often hate that I have no rice bag to wear for a long time. Old travels are like dreams, and past events are like smoke. The scenic spot is not always there, and the famous mountain has been separated. I deeply sigh that the enjoyment of happiness must be in time. (End)

Fiction Club

Women Women (15)

— Yao Sufeng

At this time, he felt that there was no way to avoid this difficulty, so he had to pretend to be serious and said in a commanding tone; "Isn't Xiao Rong over there? You don't need to call him, hurry up and pull the carriage over."

The boy was confused. He just saw Xiao Rong with a very beautiful woman, so he didn't dare to say anything more. He just went and pointed to one side and said, "The carriage is parked over there!"

At that time, Miss Ding naturally did not know what was going on, so she did not pay any attention. So Mr. Lu wanted to use the trick of getting away unnoticed, so he hurriedly walked to the other side, but Miss Ding stopped him.

"Didn't the coachman just say that the carriage was parked over there?" She pulled Mr. Lu to walk over there. Mr. Lu had no choice and could not dodge any more, so he had to follow her.

He pulled down the brim of his hat, covering half of his face, and in great panic, he had to get into his father's carriage. Fortunately, he saw that his father was dozing off in the carriage when he got in.

"Hurry up! To the Railway Hotel!" he ordered.

The boy woke Xiao Rong's father up, pulled the carriage and walked, while secretly pulling at his clothes, and pointing his mouth behind him, meaning to tell him to turn his head and see who was sitting in the carriage. But he had just woken up from his dream, and did not understand what the boy meant: but the boy still said to him softly: "Boss! Look at who is sitting behind you?"

"What's it to you? I've seen a lot of men and women from Shanghai!" Although he turned his head and took a look, he only saw Miss Ding sitting on the right. Xiao Rong happened to be sitting behind him, so he did not see it all clearly. He only thought that this was an ordinary couple.

The boy wanted to be more troublesome, but he still said softly: That's Xiao Rong!

"Don't talk nonsense! I don't have the blessing to have such a son!" He still didn't believe it, thinking that the boy was just joking with him.

The Railway Hotel arrived, and Xiao Rong quickly paid the fare and got out of the car with Miss Ding. The boy was just about to call Xiao Rong's father to see if it was Xiao Rong, when he suddenly heard someone shouting on the other side of the road: "Hurry up! Pull the carriage over!"

When he heard that business had come, he naturally did not dare to delay, so he did not have time to call Xiao Rong's father to see Xiao Rong again, and immediately pulled the carriage over.

On the road, the boy told Xiao Rong's father in detail: "The two people who took the car just now are really Xiao Rong and another woman I don't know." However, Xiao Rong's father was still skeptical and thought that he might have seen the wrong person.

Gold Market Increased by Ten Taels Last Week

Of the total of about 30,000 exchange contracts, last week's margin deposit showed signs of increasing again. However, the situation was complicated. It started weak at the beginning of the week, then turned firm, breaking through the 750 tael mark. Afterwards, it turned into a consolidation phase with twists and turns due to fluctuating international news. In total, there was a fluctuation of twenty taels, and finally, the total increase was ten taels. It seems that the market was bewildered by the conflicting international news. As for the silver market, there appeared to be a slight drop. The Shanghai exchange rate for drafts was sluggish for a long time, and it only shrank by half a grade at the end of the week. Consequently, the domestic market also tightened slightly, with forward contracts dropping within three "bian" (a unit of currency). Chinese merchants were buying to cover previous short positions, but short positions still dominate, while the gold margin spread is long. It is estimated that there are about thirty thousand exchange contracts, with spot firms and non-industry clients being mostly short, while the Dalian group is mostly long. As for spot red bars, they frequently rose last week, as the Tianjin and Dalian groups were very active. Unexpectedly, transportation was suddenly obstructed over the weekend, leading to a standstill, like a bolt from the blue. The price also fell from 13.5 taels to 11 taels (based on incremental additions to the gold margin). The gold margin, based on the daily exchange settlement price, initially suppressed 50 taels, then only 40 taels, and finally more than 40 taels, resulting in substantial profits for spot shipments. The general situation of the past week is summarized below.

There was a total fluctuation of twenty taels throughout the week. Starting on Monday (August 3rd), the gold exchange was closed for one day due to the bank holiday, but there was no rise or fall in silver or large bars. The next day, there was no market for large bars, the silver price rose by 0.125, while the forward sterling and other currencies remained unchanged. The gold market was back to normal. It opened down 4.3 "qian" (a unit of currency), at 737.5 taels, then 6.5 "qian", due to the rise in the US stock market, especially the reported rise in the silver price. Influenced by this, large investors and speculators bought in, pushing the price above 40 taels, but there were also fluctuations of three or four taels. The noon close was at 40 taels. In the afternoon, it reached 41.5 "qian", and the closing price was 39.7 "qian", a further drop of 2.1 "qian" compared to the previous Saturday. According to the whole day, the difference was five taels. On Wednesday, large bars rose by 0.0625, the silver price rose by 0.125, forward sterling remained unchanged, and the domestic market seemed loose. As for the gold margin, it opened down 2.7 "qian", at 737 taels, due to reports that cash was being transported from England to the United States, which could lead to an averaging of cash around the world, and the British exchange rate should increase. Therefore, people's hearts were withering, especially the sellers were active, and then it fell to 35.5 taels. Afterwards, due to the activation of spot shipments, it suddenly surged above the 40 tael mark. In the afternoon, the sellers softened again, and the closing price was only 36 taels, a further drop of 3.7 "qian" compared to the previous day. The next day, large bars rose again by 0.0625, the silver price by 0.125, but the external market for forward sterling remained unchanged, and the domestic market seemed slightly better. Dealers first sold and then bought in, and the gold price opened higher, at 37.2 "qian", due to the fall in the US stock market, the sharp drop in the British pound abroad, and reports that France was buying gold from the United States. As a result, the gold market was excited, large investors began to buy in, and then rose to 45.3 "qian". The market was extremely flat in the afternoon, opening at 43.2 "qian", then from four taels to 2.5 "qian", and then back to 4.5 "qian", and the closing price was 3.8 "qian", a rebound of 7.8 "qian" compared to the previous day, reversing three days of consecutive falls. The total difference for the day was 8.5 taels, with large investors demanding more than the supply, and Mr. Wu continuing to buy in. The next day, large bars contracted by 0.0625, the silver price by 0.375, forward sterling remained unchanged, but the domestic market tended to be firm, and buyers were still strong. The gold market slightly increased by one tael, to 44.8 "qian", then from 5.5 "qian" to 2.7 "qian", and then cash flowed out, and it rose to 46.2 "qian". In the afternoon, buyers were brave, and therefore especially sharp, suddenly breaking through the 50 tael mark, reaching 53.5 taels. General short positions were actively covering, and the closing price was 52.8 "qian", a further increase of nine taels compared to the previous day. In the past two days, there has been a total increase of 16.8 "qian". According to the entire market, there was a total fluctuation of 10.8 "qian". On Saturday, large bars contracted by 0.125 again, forward sterling suddenly contracted by half a grade, the domestic market was flat, Chinese merchants were buying in relentlessly, and the gold market was exactly the opposite, opening down two "qian", at 50.08 "qian", then there was a slight recovery. Yarn and Cotton - Cotton Market Initially Rose, Then Retreated Last Week

The cotton market had some upward momentum at the beginning of the week due to abnormal weather, stable foreign cotton prices, severe flooding in all directions, and increasingly severe flooding in Hankou, which was expected to have a major impact on cotton production. Therefore, domestic groups and bulls bought in and increased their positions. After a few days, the weather was still good, and the US cotton situation appeared weak again, and a downward trend suddenly started. The spot price of US cotton broke through the 8-cent mark, and there were also reports of Indian cotton being devalued and sold off. Various factories did not dare to purchase due to the uncertain general trend. As a result, people were panicked, and the price fell by eight or nine "qian" in one day. The lowest price for October was 35.6 taels. At the end of the week, due to the release of government estimates, buyers expected an upward trend, and retail investors bought in, and the market price rebounded slightly. The October price reached 36.25 taels. However, the world cotton market is very pessimistic, and it is difficult to rise sharply in the future. Therefore, large investors unanimously sold short. Buyers, on the other hand, are tight-lipped because they expect the price of gold to rise, and some even buy in to increase their positions. However, the government report released on the 8th has not yet been received in the local telegram on the 9th. US cotton alone rose slightly by 10 pounds. However, according to the Chicago telegram, the official estimate is that the cotton production is as high as 15,584,000 bales. The New York Stock Exchange was closed in the afternoon, but the Chicago Stock Exchange still had transactions as usual in the afternoon. The December price plummeted 137 points, to 6.86 cents, and the 7-cent line has been broken, which shows the extreme danger of the US cotton situation. The future of local cotton also has a very unstable phenomenon. Spot cotton trading is very cold, with 6,420 bales of Yao cotton being shipped. The amount of spot cotton that was opened is recorded on the left.

Manufacturer Price Price Transaction Time Limit

Shaanxi cotton 38.00 —— 200 pieces Spot Also

Yarn Market Fell by More Than Two Taels Last Week

Actual Sales Sharply Reduced

The yarn market moved gradually towards a soft path last week, and the situation was increasingly weak. The overseas flower and yarn situation tended to be downstream. In addition, the floods in all directions were frequent, the actual needs were greatly hit, and the various groups had no excitement. The transaction was completely stagnant, and the people were very depressed. The sellers felt active, and the big family was unmoved, and there was no idea of making up for it, because the original cotton was loose and the cost was cheaper. Buyers felt that the general situation was bad, and all the hands were unmoved. In short, the world cotton market was unusually pessimistic, and there was no revitalization. The floods in various places became more and more serious. The farmers will have weak purchasing power in autumn, so the large households unanimously sell out and look small. However, on the multi-faceted side, the attitude is still quiet because the price of gold is expected to rise, and there is no letting go. However, the current yarn transaction is too clear, and how the future will be, it must depend on the actual needs for progress and retreat. The yarn market is very weak, and there are more sellers. Each month fell by two taels from the previous week, and the transaction statistics were 29,300 bales. The current business of the guest gang is quiet, and the statistics of the various gangs in the whole week are 3,845 bales. 1,280 bales in the same industry, the market fell by two taels, and the number of bales bought by each gang is recorded below.

Foreign Cotton Before the Government Report Was Released

Yesterday, the US cotton market was waiting for the government report, and the market was mixed. First, it was firm because of the short position, and then it was weak because of the public sale. The futures rose from 5 to 11 pounds, and the spot rose from 10 pounds. British cotton futures rose from 11 to 12 points, and the spot rose from 15 points. Egyptian cotton spot rose 15 points. Indian cotton was firm due to good news from Liverpool and short position coverage, with Pingle rising 2.75 rupees, Aomula rising 3.50 rupees, and Bailuoxi rising 4.25 rupees. US Cotton Government Report Greatly Increased

Cotton Production Amount 15,584,000 bales

Chicago December Futures Plummeted to 6.86 Cents

August 8th New York Telegram: The Department of Agriculture's cotton harvest report has been released at noon today. The amount of cotton production is 15,584,000 bales, an increase of 1,500,000 bales compared to the average of various private estimates. The New York Stock Exchange will be closed on Saturday afternoon as usual, so it will have to be auctioned on Monday. The only exchange market in the United States that traded on Saturday afternoon was Chicago. After hearing the report, the December price plummeted to 6.86 cents, a drop of 137 points from the previous day.

Food: Limited Post-Market North-South Rice Market

Changxi North Japonica Rice Has Been Discontinued

New Japonica Rice Price Increases by Half a Yuan

South Market: Few sources from Luli. The trades in Qingpu No. 1, Tongli No. 2, Pinghu No. 2, and Pudong new Japonica rice No. 1 were not smooth. Because the Rice Industry Association's evaluation was public, the customers were also affected. Changxi North Japonica rice was out of stock. Early and late rice and foreign reeds were tight and the prices were slightly increasing. The rise and fall of the Su-Tong gang rice were limited. A boat of new Japonica rice arrived yesterday, with a total of more than 100 "shi" (a unit of volume). He Sheng and Shen Li bought it, and the market price rose by half a yuan compared to the previous market. Bian Yin (a type of rice) rose by two yuan. Tea shops still had strong demand, and the price increased by 0.3-0.4 yuan.

Xin Zha: Since the recent limit on the plate, the number of goods coming from the inland has been slightly less. There are about 17,000 "dan" (a unit of weight) of ship cargo in stock. In the market, the trade in Zhongguan thick japonica rice is the most, and the situation is gradually increasing. In addition, there are two kinds of top goods. Because the Rice Industry Association limits the price to 17 yuan, customers are unwilling to sell it because of the blood capital relationship. There is a lack of fresh early and late rice, and there is a slight increase in the general trend. The price of Lu Bu reed (a type of rice) is high and fixed and slightly tighter. Foreign japonica rice and Dongxin japonica rice are sold as soon as they arrive. The large market rose by half a yuan.

Silk and Tea: Silk Market Was Lonely and Uninspired Last Week

European and American Silk Telegrams Were Not Forwarded... Chinese Merchants' Attitudes Were Passive

Silk Factories Reduced Work and Stopped Machines... Silk Sales Were Extremely Sluggish

The silk market in the local foreign firms in last week was increasingly lonely and uninspired. After the summer vacation, most of the European and American silk factories have not yet started work, and the sales of raw silk factories are still stagnant. In addition, Japanese silk is still priced cheaply, and the price difference between Japanese silk and Shanghai White Factory is two or three hundred taels. Japanese merchants continue to sell hard, and no one cares about Chinese silk. The local telegrams in Shanghai were not forwarded, and both Chinese and foreign silk merchants had a passive attitude. Each silk factory's silk is getting thicker, and the types are reducing work and stopping machines. The European and American silk sales have reached their extreme. The silk market in last week has almost stagnated. The inland silk door sales are also clear, and a total of only more than 100 packs were traded in the whole week, and more than 300 packs were exported. Overseas Chinese silks are all marked with no market, and the exchange rate has decreased, and the silk price has fallen in the dark. There is really no market to record. Metals: New Lead Wire Rises Straight Up

Market Overview: Yesterday was Sunday. The metal transaction was not very good because the various gangs and factories were all resting. The city was also very idle. Because of the imports and exports of all cities, it was very small.

New Lead Wire Short and Needed: Since Dongyang lead wire cannot come to Shanghai, the Shanghai New Lead Wire market has a rising trend. The standards have been increased one after another. 16 to 20 per "dan" (unit of weight) is estimated at 13.25 taels, and 21 to 25 is sold at 18.75 taels, but the market is extremely scarce, the popularity is getting stronger, and the buyers are getting more and more prosperous, so the coming standard is expected to rise again.

Bamboo Steel Reverses from Weak to Strong: The recent purchase of bamboo steel bars is very strong, but the goods are scarce. The market has reversed from weak to strong. Each ton is sold at 95 taels. There are six or seventy tons.
